Outlet Id is ->O8180
<br>ContactId-------------C46893
<br>ContactFirstName------Jeffrey
<br>ContactMiddleName------
<br>ContactLastName-------Woldt
<br>ContactDescription----Jeffrey Woldt is Vice President and Editorial Director of Racher Press Inc. publisher of Chain Drug Review the leading source for news in the community pharmacy industry and Mass Market Retailers which reports on supermarket drug and discount retailing. In that role Woldt directs coverage of companies in those sectors and their business partners in the consumer packaged goods wholesale distribution and technology industries as well as providing commentary about emerging developments in those fields. His responsibilities include interacting with top-level executives at companies ranging from small retail chains and start-up CPG suppliers to members of the global Fortune 500 – CVS Health Walgreens Boots Alliance and Walmart among them; moderating industry forums; and hosting awards presentations.

Woldt oversees the permanent editorial staff and freelance writers and photographers and he also works closely with the art production and advertising sales departments. During the course of his career Woldt has been involved in evaluating and negotiating contacts with suppliers for editorial production technology printing and paper. He was one of a small group involved in the establishment of Racher Press’ still evolving Internet presence and is the primary point of contact for the technology services firm that maintains the company’s IT infrastructure.

Prior to joining Racher Press Woldt served as Managing Editor of Home Furnishing Daily (then owned by Fairchild Publications which also published Women’s Wear Daily) after having worked as a writer and editor at a daily newspaper in Illinois.

Outlet Id is ->O7992
<br>ContactId-------------C47102
<br>ContactFirstName------ Lakshman
<br>ContactMiddleName------J.V
<br>ContactLastName------- Rao
<br>ContactDescription----Lakshman Rao the backbone of India Tribune has been a fearless and respected journalist for over five decades. Holding a bachelor degree in economics and a post-graduate degree in journalism he started his journalistic career in Indian Railways followed by The Hitavada of Nagpur and over the years he continued to hold senior editorial positions in Deccan Chronicle of Hyderabad and Visakhapatnam in West Coast Times of Goa in various centers of Indian Express and in Express News Service New Delhi before he joined India Tribune in Chicago in 1994. He trained several budding journalists in these newspaper offices and taught journalism students at various universities including Andhra University in Visakhapatnam India and Northwestern University in Evanston USA. He visited many countries and joined the White House Press Corps accompanying President George W. Bush during his visit to India and Pakistan. Rao has published several investigative reports and highly critical articles and editorials interesting features and continues to do so. He has won many honors and awards.

<br>ContactDescription----Ruth Thompson has been involved with the Program of Legal Studies for Native People (PLSNP) in both teaching and administrative roles since 1982.  Between 1985 and 1989 she developed a skills-based curriculum for the PLSNP which had a significant impact on its success rate.  She revised the PLSNP’s substantive course content in 1993-94 to encourage law schools to give students credit for the PLSNP.She has taught international law Aboriginal law and legal writing at the U of S College of Law and has also been involved in its academic support program.  She currently team-teaches a course in international and comparative Indigenous rights with professors from universities in Canada the US Australia and New Zealand.  She supervises graduate students in Aboriginal and international law.
